SOURCEKIND_DATATYPE
public static final [String](https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/String.html) SOURCEKIND_DATATYPE
p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
For each alternatives , “source” tags depends on “kind” tags.
**TABLE**: “source” must be an instance table which is the same classifier as the “AlternativeProperty”. Sorting of rows in the table is not necessary.
**SUBTYPES**: “source” must be a parent block of subtypes which is the same type as the “AlternativeProperty”. Also, the parent block will NOT be evaluated as well as any blocks which have “Is Abstract” = true.
**EXCEL**: “source” must be a instance/generic table link to an excel file, and table columns have been mapped to excel/CSV columns. “Excel Import” plugin is required for this feature, but the user doesn’t have to use the “Read from File” menu.
See Also:
[Constant Field Values](../../../../../constant-values.html#com.nomagic.magicdraw.sysml.util.MDCustomizationForSysMLProfile.SOURCEKIND_DATATYPE)

getBlackBoxICDTable
[@Deprecated](https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html)public [Stereotype](../../../uml2/ext/magicdraw/mdprofiles/Stereotype.html) getBlackBoxICDTable()
Deprecated.
use getInstance(element).blackBoxICDTable().getStereotype()
p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
A Blackbox ICD Tablerepresents all external Ports and interfaces of the Block.
With this table you can easily:
Review interfaces (Ports) of the Block in the single place.
Customize the representation of the table.
Export the data into an *.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.
Toolbar button descriptions:
-**Delete**click to remove selected elements both from the table and from the model.
-**Remove From Table**- click to remove selected elements from the table.
-**Refresh**clickto update the contents of the table after specifying the Block.
-**Validate Diagram**clickto validate the diagram.
-**Up**click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) up a row.
-**Down**click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) down a row.
-**Show Columns**click to specify the set of columns for displaying in the table.
-**Options > Show Full Paths**click to display the full paths of elements in the table.
-**Export**- click to export the contents of the table to an*.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.
Returns:
stereotype

A parametric diagram may contain constraint properties and their parameters, along with other properties from within the internal block context. All properties that appear, other than the constraints themselves, must either be bound directly to a constraint parameter, or contain a property that is bound to one (through any number of levels of containment).

A constraint property is a property of any block that is typed by a constraint block. It holds a localized usage of the constraint block. Binding connectors may be used to bind the parameters of this constraint block to other properties of the block that contains the usage.

getPartProperty
[@Deprecated](https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html)public [Stereotype](../../../uml2/ext/magicdraw/mdprofiles/Stereotype.html) getPartProperty()
Deprecated.
use getInstance(element).partProperty().getStereotype()
A part property specifies part, with stronger ownership and coincidental lifetime, of its containing block. Every part property has 'composite' AggregationKind and is typed by a block. A part property will be displayed under the 'parts' compartment when 'Sort by SysML Style' in the 'Presentation Options' is selected. A part property describes a local usage or role of the typing block in the context of the containing block.
Returns:
stereotype

use getInstance(element).quantityKind().getStereotype()
A QuantityKind is a kind of quantity that may be stated by means of defined units. For example, the quantity kind of
 length may be measured by units of meters, kilometers, or feet. QuantityKind is defined as a stereotype of
 InstanceSpecification, but it uses this metaclass only to define supporting elements for ValueType definitions. (The reuse
 of InstanceSpecification to define another metaclass is similar to the EnumerationLiteral metaclass in UML.) The only
 valid use of a QuantityKind instance is to be referenced by the quantityKind property of a ValueType or Unit
 stereotype.
Returns:
stereotype

A Unit is a quantity in terms of which the magnitudes of other quantities that have the same dimension can be stated. A unit often relies on precise and reproducible ways to measure the unit. For example, a unit of length such as meter may be specified as a multiple of a particular wavelength of light. A unit may also specify less stable or precise ways to express some value, such as a cost expressed in some currency, or a severity rating measured by a numerical scale.

getWhiteBoxICDTable
[@Deprecated](https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html)public [Stereotype](../../../uml2/ext/magicdraw/mdprofiles/Stereotype.html) getWhiteBoxICDTable()
Deprecated.
use getInstance(element).whiteBoxICDTable().getStereotype()
p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
A Whitebox ICD Table represents assembly how Parts are connected via Ports and interfaces.
With this table you can easily:
Review Connectors of the Parts in the single place.
Customize the representation of the table.
Export the data into an *.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.
Toolbar button descriptions:
-**Delete**click to remove selected elements both from the table and from the model.
-**Remove From Table**- click to remove selected elements from the table.
-**Refresh**click<img src="mdp://resource/com/nomagic/magicdraw/icons/refresh.png" o:title="" style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;" />to update the contents of the table after specifying the Block as the context.
-**Validate Diagram**click<img src="mdp://resource/com/nomagic/magicdraw/icons/validate_diagram.png" o:title="validate_diagram" style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;" />to validate the diagram.
-**Up**click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) up a row.
-**Down**click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) down a row.
-**Show Columns**click to specify the set of columns for displaying in the table.
-**Show Parts**click to specify the set of Parts for displaying Connectors between them in the table.
-**Options > Show Full Paths**click to display the full paths of elements in the table.
-**Export**- click to export the contents of the table to an*.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.
Returns:
stereotype

<head>
<style>
 p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
 </style>
</head>
<body>
<p>
 For each   alternatives  , “source” tags depends on “kind” tags.

 </p>
<ul>
<li>
<b>TABLE</b>: “source” must be an instance table which is the same classifier as the “AlternativeProperty”. Sorting of rows in the table is not necessary.

 </li>
<li>
<b>SUBTYPES</b>: “source” must be a parent block of subtypes which is the same type as the “AlternativeProperty”. Also, the parent block will NOT be evaluated as well as any blocks which have “Is Abstract” = true.

 </li>
<li>
<b>EXCEL</b>: “source” must be a instance/generic table link to an excel file, and table columns have been mapped to excel/CSV columns. “Excel Import” plugin is required for this feature, but the user doesn’t have to use the “Read from File” menu.

 </li>
</ul>
</body>
</html></div>
<dl class="notes">
<dt>See Also:</dt>
<dd>
<ul class="see-list">
<li><a href="../../../../../constant-values.html#com.nomagic.magicdraw.sysml.util.MDCustomizationForSysMLProfile.SOURCEKIND_DATATYPE">Constant Field Values</a></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
</section>
</li>

<section class="detail" id="UNIT_QUANTITYKIND_PROPERTY">
<h3>UNIT_QUANTITYKIND_PROPERTY</h3>
<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>
</span><span class="modifiers">public static final</span> <span class="return-type"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/String.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">String</a></span> <span class="element-name">UNIT_QUANTITYKIND_PROPERTY</span></div>
<div class="deprecation-block"><span class="deprecated-label">Deprecated.</span>
<div class="deprecation-comment">use UnitStereotype.QUANTITYKIND</div>
</div>
<div class="block">A kind of quantity that may be stated by means of defined units, as identified by an instance of the Dimension stereotype. A value type may optionally specify a dimension without any unit. Such a value has no concrete representation, but may be used to express a value in an abstract form independent of any specific units.</div>

<dt>See Also:</dt>
<dd>
<ul class="see-list">
<li><a href="../../../../../constant-values.html#com.nomagic.magicdraw.sysml.util.MDCustomizationForSysMLProfile.UNIT_QUANTITYKIND_PROPERTY">Constant Field Values</a></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>

<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>

<div class="deprecation-block"><span class="deprecated-label">Deprecated.</span>
<div class="deprecation-comment">use AlternativesStereotype.SOURCE</div>
</div>
<div class="block">Source of alternatives. If the kind is specified as a Table, the source must be an Instance Table. If the kind is specified as Excel, the source must be an Instance Table linked to an Excel file or an   ImportMap   element. If the kind is specified as Subtypes, the source must be a parent Block of subtypes.</div>

<h3>getBlackBoxICDTable</h3>
<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>

<div class="block"><html>
<head>
<style>
 p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
 </style>
</head>
<body>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0cm;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">
<span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">A Blackbox ICD Table</span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">represents all external Ports and interfaces of the Block.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0cm;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">
<span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">With this table you can easily:</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Symbol;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Review interfaces (Ports) of the Block in the single place.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Symbol;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Customize the representation of the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Symbol;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Export the data into an *.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0cm;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">
<span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Toolbar button descriptions:</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Delete</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">     click to remove selected elements both from the table and from the model.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Remove From Table </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">- click to remove selected elements from the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Refresh </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click
 </span><img src="mdp://resource/com/nomagic/magicdraw/icons/refresh.png"/><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;"> to update the contents of the table after specifying the Block.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Validate Diagram </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click
 </span><img src="mdp://resource/com/nomagic/magicdraw/icons/validate_diagram.png"/><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">to validate the diagram.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Up </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) up a row.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Down</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) down a row.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-variant:normal;line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Show Columns</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to specify the set of columns for displaying in the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Options &gt; Show Full Paths </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to display the full paths of elements in the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Export</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;"> - click to export the contents of the table to an*.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.</span> 

 </p>
</body>
</html></div>
<dl class="notes">
<dt>Returns:</dt>
<dd>stereotype</dd>
</dl>
</section>
</li>

<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>

<div class="deprecation-block"><span class="deprecated-label">Deprecated.</span>
<div class="deprecation-comment">use getInstance(element).partProperty().getStereotype()</div>
</div>
<div class="block">A part property specifies part, with stronger ownership and coincidental lifetime, of its containing block. Every part property has 'composite' AggregationKind and is typed by a block. A part property will be displayed under the 'parts' compartment when 'Sort by SysML Style' in the 'Presentation Options' is selected. A part property describes a local usage or role of the typing block in the context of the containing block.</div>

<dd>stereotype</dd>

<section class="detail" id="getQuantityKind()">
<h3>getQuantityKind</h3>
<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>
</span><span class="modifiers">public</span> <span class="return-type"><a href="../../../uml2/ext/magicdraw/mdprofiles/Stereotype.html" title="interface in com.nomagic.uml2.ext.magicdraw.mdprofiles">Stereotype</a></span> <span class="element-name">getQuantityKind</span>()</div>
<div class="deprecation-block"><span class="deprecated-label">Deprecated.</span>
<div class="deprecation-comment">use getInstance(element).quantityKind().getStereotype()</div>
</div>
<div class="block">A QuantityKind is a kind of quantity that may be stated by means of defined units. For example, the quantity kind of
 length may be measured by units of meters, kilometers, or feet. QuantityKind is defined as a stereotype of
 InstanceSpecification, but it uses this metaclass only to define supporting elements for ValueType definitions. (The reuse
 of InstanceSpecification to define another metaclass is similar to the EnumerationLiteral metaclass in UML.) The only
 valid use of a QuantityKind instance is to be referenced by the    quantityKind    property of a ValueType or Unit
 stereotype.</div>
<dl class="notes">
<dt>Returns:</dt>
<dd>stereotype</dd>
</dl>
</section>
</li>

<section class="detail" id="getUnit()">
<h3>getUnit</h3>
<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>
</span><span class="modifiers">public</span> <span class="return-type"><a href="../../../uml2/ext/magicdraw/mdprofiles/Stereotype.html" title="interface in com.nomagic.uml2.ext.magicdraw.mdprofiles">Stereotype</a></span> <span class="element-name">getUnit</span>()</div>
<div class="deprecation-block"><span class="deprecated-label">Deprecated.</span>
<div class="deprecation-comment">use getInstance(element).unit().getStereotype()</div>
</div>
<div class="block">A Unit is a quantity in terms of which the magnitudes of other quantities that have the same dimension can be stated. A unit often relies on precise and reproducible ways to measure the unit. For example, a unit of length such as meter may be specified as a multiple of a particular wavelength of light. A unit may also specify less stable or precise ways to express some value, such as a cost expressed in some currency, or a severity rating measured by a numerical scale.</div>
<dl class="notes">
<dt>Returns:</dt>
<dd>stereotype</dd>
</dl>
</section>

<li>
<section class="detail" id="getWhiteBoxICDTable()">
<h3>getWhiteBoxICDTable</h3>
<div class="member-signature"><span class="annotations"><a class="external-link" href="https://docs.oracle.com/en/java/javase/17/docs/api/java.base/java/lang/Deprecated.html" title="class or interface in java.lang">@Deprecated</a>
</span><span class="modifiers">public</span> <span class="return-type"><a href="../../../uml2/ext/magicdraw/mdprofiles/Stereotype.html" title="interface in com.nomagic.uml2.ext.magicdraw.mdprofiles">Stereotype</a></span> <span class="element-name">getWhiteBoxICDTable</span>()</div>
<div class="deprecation-block"><span class="deprecated-label">Deprecated.</span>
<div class="deprecation-comment">use getInstance(element).whiteBoxICDTable().getStereotype()</div>
</div>
<div class="block"><html>
<head>
<style>
 p {padding:0px; margin:0px;}
 </style>
</head>
<body>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0cm;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">
<span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">A Whitebox ICD Table represents assembly     how Parts are connected via Ports and interfaces.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0cm;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">
<span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">With this table you can easily:</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Symbol;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Review Connectors of the Parts in the single place.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Symbol;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Customize the representation of the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Symbol;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Export the data into an *.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:0cm;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;">
<span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Toolbar button descriptions:</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Delete</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">     click to remove selected elements both from the table and from the model.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Remove From Table </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">- click to remove selected elements from the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Refresh </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click
 </span><span>&lt;img src="mdp://resource/com/nomagic/magicdraw/icons/refresh.png" o:title="" style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;" /&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;"> to update the contents of the table after specifying the Block as the context.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Validate Diagram </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click
 </span><span>&lt;img src="mdp://resource/com/nomagic/magicdraw/icons/validate_diagram.png" o:title="validate_diagram" style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;" /&gt;</span><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">to validate the diagram.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Up </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) up a row.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Down</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to shift selected elements (either grouped or non-grouped) down a row.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-variant:normal;line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Show Columns</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to specify the set of columns for displaying in the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-variant:normal;line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-weight:normal; font-family:Times New Roman;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Show Parts</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">     click to specify the set of Parts for displaying Connectors between them in the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Options &gt; Show Full Paths </span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">    click to display the full paths of elements in the table.</span>
</p>
<p style="margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:10.0pt;margin-left:36.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Calibri,sans-serif;text-indent:-18.0pt;">
<span style="font-family:Cambria,serif;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;">-</span><span style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-weight:normal;;font-variant:normal; line-height:normal;"> </span><b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">Export</span></b><span style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;"> - click to export the contents of the table to an*.html, *.csv, or *.xlsx file.</span> 

 </p>
</body>
</html></div>
<dl class="notes">

<dd>stereotype</dd>
